//  ==========================================================================================================================
//
//  AI Profile name:
//
//    Acid (momentary derivative placeholder until actual profile is developed)
//
//      This AI profile is designed for Total Annihilation: Escalation and includes units content introduced up to v9.2
//      That means AI does NOT build tier 4 content because that tier did not exist until Escalation v9.5+
//
//      However, this profile is NOT compatible with Escalation v9.2 because 9.2 requires customized AI UnitNames for Wotan's
//      prototype directional build-plate factories within v9.2 for player while AI had to build different factory UnitIDs.
//      For example, player builds ARMSY/ARMFHP while AI must build ARMSY_AI/ARMFHP_AI.  A profile version compatible with
//      Escalation v9.2 is in "AI Profiles Pack v2020.04.30b for Escalation 9.2" available for download at:
//        https://www.tauniverse.com/forum/showthread.php?t=46159
//
//
//  Version: 1.0b
//  Release date: April 25, 2020 updated September 30, 2022 to be compatible with Escalation v9.3 through 9.9.2
//
//  Details about this version:
//
//    a) For maps with starting positions separated by spotty/limited use of land/water traversable by AI hovercraft
//
//    b) DOES NOT BUILD SHIPS or submerged structures other than Underwater Metal/Moho Extractors.  This profile is designed
//       for land maps, including land maps having significant amount of water unsuitable for AI shipbuilding (such as small
//       lakes/ponds).
//
//    c) Does NOT build Escalation AI cheat units
//
//    d) Builds long range artillery (terrain permitting) using following limits according to game difficulty setting:
//
//                                             Easy    Medium    Hard
//         Arm Big Bertha / Core Intimidator     0        2        4
//         Arm Vulcan / Core Buzzsaw             0        1        2  <-- Units retired in Esc v9.1.1 then revived v9.8.5
//         Arm Armageddon / Core Dictator        0        1        2
//
//         The above nonzero artillery values can be exceeded because game engine does not count incomplete buildings when
//         tallying unit quantities throughout a game.  That quirk is a consideration in chosen values, above.
//
//  This profile being derived from Escalation v9.2 era will have variable availability of Arm Orion, Ambusher, Vulcan and
//  Core Viper, Toaster, Buzzsaw.  Those units were retired in Escalation v9.1.1 then later revived in v9.8.5.
//
//
//  "Standby" mode detrimental stall caused by submerged content:
//
//    An AI controlled mobile combat unit can temporarily stall in Standby mode on maps with water when nearest enemy unit
//    is not targetable by the combat unit's weapon(s).  Standby mode can linger until non-targetable unit is destroyed or
//    a targetable enemy unit moves closer.  Some examples of the stall include:
//
//    - mobile land unit fixating on a submerged unit (Wotan and Admiral_94 have improved this within Escalation during 2021)
//    - hovercraft without depth charge/torpedo fixating on a submerged unit
//    - submerged amphibious unit without torpedo fixating on a floating unit
//    - ships without depth charge/torpedo fixating on a submerged unit
//    - submarine fixating on a hovercraft unit
//
//    This stall has existed in varying degrees since Total Annihilation's birth.  Its frequency increases as amount of
//    submerged units increases.  The following list shows some significant plateaus.
//
//      Total Annhilation Version      Number of Submerged Units
//
//      Total Annihilation v3.1c          5
//      Core Contingency expansion       15
//      Escalation Beta v8.9             23
//      Escalation Gold v9.7             41 (53 when including submerged amphibious)
//
//    Standby mode stall is related to game engine's limited handling of AI targets.  A tendency of an AI mobile combat unit
//    to focus on nearest enemy unit even when weapon(s) can not deal with that enemy unit.  Stall frequency would improve if
//    engine supported AI unit cycling to second, third, fourth or fifth nearest enemy unit before resorting to Standby mode.
//
//
//  Author: TAfan97
//
//    Can be messaged via Total Annihilation Universe forum private messaging at:
//      https://www.tauniverse.com/forum/member.php?u=24519
//    Generally, higher Escalation AI development activity during Canadian winters and can be on hiatus outside of those
//    months.  Since number of AI profiles has ballooned to eleven+ since Escalation v9.2, majority of my maintenance
//    updates will involve the more worthwhile land AI profiles (ie. DEFAULT, Urban) to maximize value from available
//    development time.
//
//  ==========================================================================================================================


// Play tests and data mining included content within:

// - Escalation v9.1.0_Test_36
// - Escalation v9.1.0_Test_37
// Except where specifically noted, unit/weapon data detailed in this AI profile are values from test releases listed above


//  Arm/Core COMMON SECTION applies to Easy/Medium/Hard difficulty

// Following two default weights can be lower but do not fall below 0.02 otherwise Commander stuck in Standby at game start,
// instead, can use Limit 0 for AI to avoid undefined units
Weight ARM 0.2
Weight CORE 0.2
// If there are duplicate nondefault Limit while default Limit exists then TA uses default Limit
// If there are duplicate nondefault Limit while default Limit nonexistent then TA uses first (topmost) Limit
Limit ARM 0
Limit CORE 0

// T1:

// "ARM/CORDPL = Depthcharge VTOL Bombers" - AI able to effectively sustain attack hovering above submerged target

// Zephyr (Depthcharge Bomber)  wpri_BadTargetCategory=NSHP  BadTargetCategory=NSHP  NoChaseCategory=AIR

// when long range artillery, both land and naval combat:                      250,000 hard / 150,000 medium / 100,000 easy
// when long range artillery, no naval combat:                                 200,000 hard / 100,000 medium /  50,000 easy
// when long range artillery, no mobile land weapons (limited land/artillery): 150,000 hard / 100,000 medium /  50,000 easy
// when no long range artillery, has land and naval combat:                    150,000 hard / 100,000 medium /  50,000 easy
// when no long range artillery, no naval combat:                              100,000 hard /  50,000 medium /  25,000 easy
// when no long range artillery, no mobile land weapons (limited land):         80,000 hard /  40,000 medium /  20,000 easy
// when land construction unavailable:                                          60,000 hard /  30,000 medium /  15,000 easy
// Plus: Arm needs extra 1 SFUS per 1 FORGE; Arm/Core need 1 SFUS per 5 SHGEN

//
// Resource Generator when making 2 metal during hard difficulty yields 0 energy.  However, on medium difficulty produces
// 1.4 metal while draining 75 energy, and easy gives 1 metal while draining 125 energy.  Although less rewarding for AI
// during medium and easy difficulty, Resource Generator still play tested to be useful for all difficulty levels.
// Following unit is supplemented by UWMFUS for energy but not metal making
// Limit CORGEN 1  // Boosted from v9.0.0 value helping compensate for less energy output per generator

// buildable by Commander to avoid it wandering long distances to build them.  However, the only water based antiaircraft
// structure (FRT) is buildable by Commander unless Sidedata.tdf is customized to avoid it.  Maps with small bodies of water
// increase risk of these structures blocking units exiting floating hovercraft plants.  Also, small ponds have possibility

// Experimental Fusion Reactor during hard difficulty outputs 5,000 energy, medium 3,500, easy 2,500
Limit CORSFUS 1
//
// Escalation v8.9.0 CORSFUS_UPGRADE bug observed 20181125 on metal seabed map (Seven Islands map within Totala2.hpi).
// CORSFUS_UPGRADE was seen as the very last standing AI units (2 of them) not yet destroyed and still "under construction"
// on the metal seabed with no associated CORSFUS.  Attacking forces were unable to target them after destroying all other
// units belonging to that AI.  Its location appeared on minimap.  Command "+view" was used to reveal it.  Escalation v9.0.0
// CORSFUS_UPGRADE.bos is identical to v8.9.0.  SFUS_UPGRADE limit 0 (while SFUS.fbi using "Builder=0") allowed 20191114
// play tests to get past 2 consecutive Game Time ~1:00:00 crashes due to:
//   Instruction pointer is 0040BD41
//   ExceptionCode = C0000005 - Access Violation
//   Access violation: Illegal read, data address 0x03307DB0
//
// SFUS_UPGRADE limit is intentionally higher than SFUS limit to allow any extras to be upgraded
Limit CORSFUS_UPGRADE 99
//
// Unlike its Arm counterpart, CORSHGEN does not have an upgrade version
Limit CORSHGEN 10
